Notes: 
------
The commited SVN version of this file will always be different from the SVN log. The latest version will be synced after being published.
This file will be updated when Panza is released, and may not contain log entries between releases during development.
This is a copy of the SVN log for Panza. Missing sequence numbers are updates for other addons in the trunk path on SVN.

Priest Logic:
HOT="Renew"
Flash=InSpellBook("FLASH") ? "FLASH" : "LESSERHEAL";
Heal=InSpellBOok("GreaterHeal") ? "GREATERHEAL" : "HEAL";

IF (InSpellBook(HOT) and BuffNotFound(HOT)) then
 spell=HOT
Elseif (FLASH Selection as per tooltips)
 If Mana >= FLASH rank 1 then
  spell=FLASH
 else
  spell="LESSERHEAL"
 end
elseif (InSpellBook(Heal)) then
 spell=HEAL
else
 spell="LESSERHEAL"
end
